### C-029: "Today Is Septima's Birthday." — May 3 Heritage Anchor (Mother of the Movement)
- **Story Source:** Cultural Moment (Septima Clark birthday May 3, 1898 — 128 years today) + Industry Commentary (Black women teachers as the unnamed engine of the Civil Rights Movement)
- **Emotional Driver:** Reverence → Pride → Decisive Joy ("we owe her enough to know her name")
- **Hook (Hot Dog) — 3 angles:**
  - **A1 (the name first):** "Today is Septima Clark's 128th birthday. You probably don't know her name. Martin Luther King Jr. did. He called her *the Mother of the Movement.*"
  - **A2 (the Rosa Parks reveal):** "Before Rosa Parks refused to give up her seat in 1955, she sat in a classroom. The woman teaching the class was Septima Clark. Today is Septima's 128th birthday. Most of us don't know her name."
  - **A3 (the math):** "Septima Clark, Charleston, born May 3, 1898. By 1965 her Citizenship Schools had registered approximately 700,000 Black voters across the Deep South. She did the work that made the marches possible. The marches got the photos. She got the work."
- **Bridge (5-beat):**
  1. **Septima context (in scene — Michelle reads the Wikipedia entry):** Born Charleston SC, 1898. Worked as a teacher 40 years. Fired in 1956 for refusing to leave the NAACP. Founded the Citizenship Schools at Highlander Folk School in 1954. Trained the women who trained the women who trained Rosa Parks. MLK called her *the Mother of the Movement.* History calls her almost nothing.
  2. **The quote that lands (verbatim, preserved):** *"Literacy means liberation."* Then: *"Don't ever think that everything went right. It didn't. Many times there were failures. But we had to mull over those failures and work until we could get them ironed out."* Then the line that did NOT make it onto the postage stamp: women's unequal treatment was *"one of the greatest weaknesses of the civil rights movement."* — Septima Clark, on the men she made.
  3. **The Mother's Day TURN (Sunday-to-Sunday):** "Today is Sunday. Next Sunday is Mother's Day. The mother in your house. The one who raised you. The one you ARE. Today the calendar gave us a fourth: the mother of the movement that made the women in your house possible. Septima taught hundreds of teachers, who taught thousands of voters, who voted in Black congresswomen, who passed the laws that let your mother walk into a department store and try on a leather bag without explanation."
  4. **The brand-as-receipt frame (light):** "Sunday to Sunday. One week from today. The bag you're choosing for her is small math. Septima's math was bigger. We owe her enough to know her name. Knowing her name is free. Calling out a Black-owned bag for the mother in your life is a different kind of receipt."
  5. **CTA + close:** Heritage Tote / Imarimom / Godfidence — heritage-anchored SKU choice. 60% off MD2026 + Express May 7-8 (only lane that lands before next Sunday) reality. Close: *"Septima Clark, Charleston, May 3, 1898. The grandmother of the movement that made you possible. Happy birthday, Septima. Next Sunday is for your daughters."*
- **Product (Broccoli):** Heritage Tote OR Imarimom OR Godfidence — single named SKU, heritage-anchored. 60% off MD2026 + Express May 7-8 only safe lane (per R-039 today's reality — Standard May 9-12 might land ON or after MD). NO multi-SKU push. NO listicle.
- **Character:**
  - **Michelle** solo POV (reads, sits, recognizes the unnamed engine, writes)
  - **Septima Clark** (in 3 verbatim-quote beats — *"Literacy means liberation"* + the failures-quote + the women's-unequal-treatment-quote. NO impersonation, NO scene reconstruction. Honor via direct quotation.)
  - **Rosa Parks** (1-line beat — "sat in Septima's classroom before she sat on the bus" — verify Highlander attendance, factual)
  - **MLK** (1-line beat — "called her the Mother of the Movement," verify attribution)
  - ⚠️ **NO George/Alice/Marcus/Keisha/Tasha/Nia** — heritage anchor = Michelle solo, matches R-033 register
  - ⚠️ **NO product-team cameo** — let the historical figures carry the room
- **Throughline:** Septima Clark made the women who made the women who made Mother's Day worth honoring. Today is her 128th birthday. Most of us don't know her name. Sunday we change that.
- **Subject Line Ideas:**
  - "Today is Septima's 128th birthday."
  - "Before Rosa sat down, Septima taught her."
  - "MLK called her the Mother of the Movement."
  - "You probably don't know her name."
  - "Literacy means liberation. — Septima Clark, May 3, 1898."
  - "The woman who taught Rosa Parks."
  - "Charleston, 1898."
  - "Today is Sunday. Septima was born on a Sunday too." (verify day-of-week 1898 if used)
  - "Next Sunday is for her daughters."
- **Preview Line Ideas:**
  - "She trained the women who trained Rosa Parks."
  - "700,000 Black voters by 1965. Most of us don't know her name."
  - "She got the work. The marches got the photos."
  - "Sunday is for her daughters."
- **Structure:**
  1. Cold open (one of A1/A2/A3 — name + birthday + MLK title)
  2. Septima context beat (Charleston, teacher, fired, Citizenship Schools, ~700K voters)
  3. 3 verbatim quotes (Literacy means liberation + failures-quote + women's-unequal-treatment quote)
  4. Mother's Day TURN (today the calendar gave us a fourth mother)
  5. Brand-as-receipt beat (light, NOT lecture)
  6. CTA (Heritage Tote/Imarimom/Godfidence + Express only lane)
  7. Close ("Septima Clark, Charleston, May 3, 1898. Happy birthday. Sunday is for your daughters.")
- **Missing:** Decide R-033 vs C-029 conflict — is C-029 R-033's reframe (Septima for May 3 birthday-on-the-day vs Emma Clement May 9 MD-eve heritage)? Or do BOTH ship (C-029 May 03 daily + R-033 May 09 Saturday)? If both ship, watch for heritage-anchor compounding within W19 — pair only if the Saturday Emma email reframes via the "Septima trained the women who carried Emma's torch" through-line. User direction needed.
- **⚠️ Watchouts:**
  - 🔴 **Heritage anchor compounding risk with R-033 Emma Clement May 9.** Both are "Black woman heritage figure + Mother's Day frame." If both ship in W19, the second one feels like a quiz. Mitigation paths: (a) Pick ONE for May 03 vs May 09. (b) If both ship, R-033 Emma reframes to "Septima taught the women who taught the women who taught Emma's grandchildren — the line is older than the prize." (c) Defer C-029 to next May 3 (2027) OR Black History Month 2027 (Feb 2027).
  - 🔴 **Verify Septima Clark facts before publish** — birthday May 3, 1898 ✓ (confirmed Wikipedia + Women's History) · MLK "Mother of the Movement" attribution ✓ · Rosa Parks attended Highlander workshops pre-Bus-Boycott ✓ (KingInstitute Stanford + multiple sources) · ~700K voters figure ✓ (multiple sources) · ALL three quotes verbatim from primary or near-primary sources before publish (Wikipedia + Children's Defense Fund + AAIHS).
  - 🟡 **Heavy material — needs `/review-brand` heavy attention.** Same caveat as R-033. Don't ship in a sale-push slot. Frame = HONOR via direct quotation, NOT "use her image to sell bags."
  - 🟡 **The "men she made" quote is sharp.** Septima's *"women's unequal treatment was one of the greatest weaknesses of the civil rights movement"* line is included DELIBERATELY — it lands the email's spine (the unnamed women carrying movements without credit). But it's confrontational. Let the quote do the work; don't editorialize.
  - 🟡 **Brand-as-receipt beat must NOT overreach.** "Calling out a Black-owned bag" is the soft frame. Don't equate buying a handbag with civil rights work. Septima registered voters; Afroyla sells bags. The connection is "the women she made possible exist now and Mother's Day is for them" — NOT "your purchase is activism."
  - 🟢 **Heritage value explicit** ✓ (entire email IS heritage, on her actual birthday)
  - 🟢 **Female rebalance** ✓ (Michelle solo + Septima + Rosa + MLK 1-line credit beat)
  - 🟢 **Boldness preserved** ✓ ("we owe her enough to know her name")
- **Source:** [Septima Clark Wikipedia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Septima_Poinsette_Clark) + [Stanford King Institute — Septima Clark](https://kinginstitute.stanford.edu/clark-septima-poinsette) + [SNCC Digital Gateway — Septima Clark](https://snccdigital.org/people/septima-clark/) + [TIME — How Septima Clark Schooled Civil Rights](https://time.com/4213751/septima-clark-civil-rights-movement/) + [Women's History — Bessie Coleman & May Anniversaries](https://www.womenshistory.org/education-resources/biographies/bessie-coleman) + [AAIHS — Septima Clark](https://www.aaihs.org/septima-clark-an-unsung-hero-in-the-fight-for-civil-rights/) + [Children's Defense Fund — Honoring Septima Clark](https://www.childrensdefense.org/honoring-septima-clark/)

### C-028: "Two May Firsts: Emma 1946 + Gwendolyn 1950" — Paired Heritage Frame
- **Story Source:** Cultural Moment (heritage anchor pair) + Industry Commentary (visibility-then-vs-now compression)
- **Emotional Driver:** Pride → Reverence → Decisive Joy
- **Hook (Hot Dog):** "Two May Firsts. Same week, four years apart. Both Black women. Both told the world they existed by being named for the first time."
- **Bridge:**
  1. **May 1, 1946 — Emma Clarissa Clement** named American Mother of the Year by the Golden Rule Foundation. Granddaughter of a slave. 71yo. Accepted *"in the name of millions of Negroes in the United States, and in the name of all mothers."*
  2. **May 1, 1950 — Gwendolyn Brooks** wins the Pulitzer Prize for Poetry for *Annie Allen* — book of poems about a Black girl growing up + her mother. First African American to win a Pulitzer in any category. The detail: she was getting ready to take her **9-year-old son Hank to a movie** when the reporter called with the news.
  3. **The compression beat:** Four years apart. Same first week of May. Two Black women — one a mother, one a poet writing about mothers — got named publicly for the first time.
  4. **The TURN:** Eighty years between Emma Clement walking off that stage and a Black woman in 2026 hitting "add to cart" on a leather bag with a Black silhouette stitched into it. Seventy-six years between Gwendolyn Brooks taking Hank to the movies after winning a Pulitzer and a Black mother in 2026 reading her son a story before bed. **The math is closer than it feels.**
  5. **CTA + close:** Heritage Tote / Imarimom / Godfidence — heritage-anchored SKU choice. Close: *"In the name of all mothers. Including the one in your house. Including the one who raised you. Including the one you are."* (Same close as R-033 — could merge.)
- **Product (Broccoli):** Heritage Tote OR Imarimom OR Godfidence — single named SKU. 60% off MD2026 + shipping window pivot.
- **Character:** Michelle solo POV (reads both stories, holds the compression) · Emma Clarissa Clement (1946 speech beat) · Gwendolyn Brooks (taking Hank to a movie beat — humanizing detail) · NO team cameos
- **Missing:** Decide R-033 vs C-028 conflict — is C-028 R-033's reframe, or a separate W20+ post-MD heritage essay? If R-033 stays solo Emma → C-028 becomes alternative-W20-anchor. If R-033 absorbs Gwendolyn → C-028 archived/merged.
- **⚠️ Watchouts:**
  - 🟡 **Two-figure heritage email risks splitting reverence** — could read as "history quiz" rather than honoring. Best test: Michelle's POV must connect emotionally to ONE of them and let the other resonate by proximity. Don't double-narrate.
  - 🟡 **Verify Gwendolyn Brooks Pulitzer 1950 + son Hank + movie detail** before send. Annie Allen contents per Wikipedia + The Morgan Library + Britannica.
  - 🟢 **Heritage value explicit** ✓
  - 🟢 **Female rebalance** ✓
- **Source:** [Annie Allen — Wikipedia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Annie_Allen) + [Gwendolyn Brooks — Britannica](https://www.britannica.com/biography/Gwendolyn-Brooks) + [Emma C. Clement 1946 — American Mothers](https://www.americanmothers.org/blog/blog/1946-national-mother-of-the-year) + [Emma C. Clement Wikipedia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emma_C._Clement) — pairs with R-033 (parent entry)
- **Added:** 2026-05-03

  >

Frame is RECEIPT-DELIVERY ("you asked, we built, here it is") not new-launch-hype.

  - **3-question verbatim burst with TURN-as-synthesis** — single-line TURN ("did I click in time?") carries the email's emotional payload + speaks for every late-clicker on the list.

  - **6 ruthless cuts** = 14% leaner email (~510 → ~440 words) without losing emotional content. Trust the reader to do their own math.
  - **Tasha→Jennifer canon restoration** caught by /review-brand — Tasha is sale-day-only Hype Woman (NOT customer support); Jennifer is canonical CS NPC.
- **Reusable patterns harvested:**
  - **Stakes-first declaration cold open** for deadline-adjacent emails (variant on customer-voice cold open mechanic) — Tier-1 reusable
  - **Customer-voice-cascade-as-confirmation pattern** (vs customer-voice cold open) — both validated
  - **3-question verbatim burst with TURN-as-synthesis** — for any customer email with multiple questions
  - **Buffer-not-wall framing** for deadline-content fatigue mitigation in 4+ consecutive deadline-adjacent email sequences
  - **Airport-countdown simile + worst-case-scenario inhabit** as narrative-copywriting replacement for shipping-math lists
  - **Inline product image as gift-suggestion answer** — first daily mechanic, watch click attribution before declaring Tier-1
  - **Sunday-morning sit-still beat** — gift-as-product reaction beat template
  - **Imani-as-example reframing** ("[product] is one bag. [N] others on the page. yours might want different.") — single-product highlight that shouldn't suppress broader catalog
  - **P.S. service-recovery acknowledgment with canonical CS NPC deferral** (Jennifer-from-Support)
- **Strategic Watchouts Carried Forward:**

  - V1 essay (3-quote opener Solomon→Elias→Ben): user rejected hook framing — wanted simpler announcement

  - Project-launch announcement opener landed user direction ("nhiệt huyết hơn vui vẻ hơn... giới thiệu 1 dự án mới")
  - Early CTA-with-explicit-feedback-ask resolved confusion that "Peek at the sketches" gallery framing created
  - "A year. A WHOLE YEAR." + "year of soon" 3-word landing beat = comedic engine + emotional payoff
  - Solomon "called me sister" punchline + Elias "haven't heard 'Dope' since 2007. Welcome back, gentlemen." reaction beat balanced fun-density across Section 2

  - Math caught by /review-brand before publish (would have been mocked by careful readers — "Michelle's math is off by a week")
  - Double-entendre caught by /review-brand before publish (audience-respect avoidable risk removed)

  - Hook: 3-quote essay opener → "Sisters. Got news." simple announcement (user direction)

  - Early CTA: absent (V1) → bare button (V4) → button-with-explicit-feedback-setup (V8)
  - Math: "8 weeks from Sunday" (V1-V6) → "7 weeks from Sunday" (V7+, /review-brand catch)
  - Tone: "the men are coming" (V6) → "Welcome back, gentlemen." (V7+, double-entendre fix)
  - Keisha: "we're not WOW'd" (V6) → "she's not WOW'd either" (V7+, attribution rescue)
  - HR rules: 4 (V5) → 3 (V6+, dropped pre-Father's-Day rule for smoother seam)
  - Length: ~445 (V3) → ~510 (V6) → ~535 (V8 with feedback-ask setup)
- **Time to Approve:** Nhiều (8 vòng) — driven by 4 user-direction redirects (English language fix, George reframe, project-launch tone, early CTA clarity) + 3 review-agent passes catching real issues (copywriter tics, math error, double-entendre)
- **Reusable patterns harvested:**
  - **Project-launch announcement opener** — "Sisters. Got news. After X years of [Y], finally [Z]." — works for any new product line / collection / service launch
  - **Year-of-soon landing beat** — 3-word emotional anchor after a sustained complaint thread ("A year of soon.")
  - **Early-CTA-with-explicit-feedback-ask** — when CTA is a feedback/survey link, explain WHAT clicking does + WHAT the reader gives ("tell us which ones land") to avoid gallery-preview ambiguity
  - **Welcome-back-gentlemen warm micro-beat** — for emails about/around male readers in a primarily-female-audience brand, brief acknowledgment closes the loop without alienating core audience
  - **Character-canon-extension via emotional state** — oblivious George can become exasperated George under sustained frustration without breaking canon (defensible character growth, not contradiction)
  - **3-customer-voice cluster as demand validation** — Solomon/Elias/(cut Ben) verbatim quotes establish pattern over single anecdote, supports community-co-creation ask
  - **Honest-not-polished founder vulnerability** — "we're not WOW'd yet" admission earns trust + invites participation more than confident reveal

- **Segment:** MASS (~193K) — W18 Day 1, post-MD-sale recovery week, MD May 10 = 13 days out
- **Theme:** Daily — Industry Commentary (zoomed out — phenomenon, not person) + Michelle's World + soft MD-shipping pivot. No Campaign Job.
- **Origin:** R-025 — created same session via `/idea-research` Apr 27 audit of cultural moment around Black women prioritizing career over family (Emma Grede WSJ Apr 4 + Breakfast Club + Today show). Promoted CONCEPT → R-025 → USED in single chain.
- **Approach:** "Sitcom dialog with George as audience surrogate" — A3 polarization-aware curiosity-gap hook ("Some of you are going to hate this email") + Michelle/George kitchen sitcom delivers full 5W1H about the Emma Grede phenomenon through George's clueless-husband questions ("Should I know her" / "What does that mean" / "What's a core memory") — exposition without lecture. Michelle's reflection lands "different math, both valid" frame (career-prioritizing women + no-choice-math majority both honored). Calendar pivot via "Where's the bag, Michelle" George demand → Michelle's calendar glance → 60% OFF + May 1 cutoff lands IN dialog. Meta-reveal beat ("That you just told me?") + George 4th-wall P.S. ("max three-hour husband" inversion — "what would I even DO with the other 165 hours").
- **Characters:** Michelle POV (reading phone, sitcom partner, calendar glance pivot) · George (full sitcom partner — bald, clueless-sweet, audience surrogate via questions, accidental wisdom on close, 4th-wall P.S.). NO Keisha/Marcus/Tasha/Alice/Nia (correct density preservation).
- **Iterations:** 5 versions across 3 review rounds
  - V1 essay: rejected by user as "không phải dạng intereactive như thông thường" — too academic
  - V3 reframe: phenomenon-as-window, không name-drop ai (Emma OR Coretta/Morrison/Angelou) — đối xứng rule
  - Hook brainstorm: 4 curiosity-gap openings (A1 closed-laptop / A2 number-floats / A3 hate-love-find-out / A4 doubling-down) → user pick A3 (polarization-aware, brand-aligned)
  - V4 craft REWRITE: voice failed essay-mode → sitcom dialog with George + full 5W1H Emma context delivered through George's clueless questions
  - V5 craft patch: rhythm fix (less fragmentation, fuller sentences in narration, dialogue stays clipped) + Emma intro trim (~50 words → ~25 words, dropped name-dropping) + EXPANDED 3-hour-mom + core-memory explanations (~15 words → ~70 + ~80 words)
  - V5.1 craft patch: bridge sentence ("told George I was about to sit down and write today's email about it") + meta-reveal beat ("That you just told me?") to land "what's the email about" naturally
- **Review agents:** craft ×3 rounds (REWRITE → 2 patches) + strategy 🟡 GOOD-BUT-CAN-BE-STRONGER (user OVERRIDE) + brand ⚠️ FIX-BEFORE-PUBLISH 4 issues (user OVERRIDE)
- **Override notes:**
  - Strategy concerns logged: centrist "neither one is wrong" landing dilutes Industry Commentary stance-taking · word-budget Emma 60% / Reader 25% backwards vs throughline · tonal whiplash from Apr 26 Reggie customer-voice register
  - Brand concerns logged: George ~50% body word count for non-sale daily stretches "primarily P.S./P.P.S." cast rule (precedent set — flag if next 3-4 dailies pull George into body too) · "So she's parenting based on a cartoon" too witty for George canon (he misobserves, doesn't punchline) · "the other 165 hours" math too accurate for George ("I thought SEO meant Super Excellent Offer" character) · "kid will know" beat could wound no-choice-math audience (recommended add no-choice-clarification — not applied) · brand values Heritage/Self-investment/Quality absent + Boldness undermined by centrist landing · greeting absence (intentional cold-open OR violation — undecided, lean intentional)
- **Reusable patterns harvested:**
  - **Sitcom dialog as 5W1H delivery vehicle:** clueless-husband (George) audience surrogate asks questions Michelle answers — reader gets exposition through DIALOGUE instead of lecture. Best for Industry Commentary topics requiring significant external setup.
  - **A3 polarization-aware hook:** "Some of you are going to hate this email. Some are going to love it. Let's find out together." — reader self-selects in. Brand-aligned with "polarization is essential."
  - **George "Where's the bag" pivot:** when Michelle's been on a tangent, have George demand the bag/CTA explicitly → Michelle's body-action response (calendar glance) becomes the pivot bridge. Better than naked transition.
  - **Meta-reveal beat:** "That you just told me?" — works when the email IS the conversation Michelle is describing. Daniel-Throssell-style 4th-wall move.
  - **Phenomenon-as-window, not person-as-target:** treat the PHENOMENON as the story (the thing many women do/face), the PERSON as the news vehicle. Reduces brand attack-surface, scales to future similar moments.
- **Performance:** *TBD — open/click + CTA click-through metrics pending. Watch: opens (predicted high — A3 hook + sitcom format), CTR (predicted lower than Rita baseline — soft buried CTA), reply rate (predicted high — defensive replies expected from career-prioritizing readers), unsubscribe rate (watch for spike → would confirm "kid will know" beat or IC register was wrong call).*
- **Hygiene TODO:** None. George main-body usage flagged for pattern-watch (if next 3-4 dailies repeat = template drift).

---

## ID Convention

- S-001, S-002... cho SEED
- C-001, C-002... cho CONCEPT
- R-001, R-002... cho READY
- U-001, U-002... cho USED
- Khi promote: S-005 → C-005 → R-005 → U-005 (giữ nguyên số)
